[26] system_message (background-consult):

const headingData1 = await page.locator('main h2').evaluateAll(hs => hs.map((h,i)=>{
  const card = h.closest('[class*="ProductCard"], [class*="product-card"], li, article, .pd03-product-card, [data-testid], div') || h.parentElement;
  let node = h;
  for (let d=0; d<8 && node; d++, node=node.parentElement) {
    const text = node.innerText || '';
    if (/\$[\d,]+\.\d{2}/.test(text) && text.length < 2000) { card = node; break; }
  }
  const text = card?.innerText || '';
  const links = [...(card?.querySelectorAll('a[href]')||[])].map(a=>({text:a.innerText.trim(), href:a.href, aria:a.getAttribute('aria-label')}));
  return {i, h:h.innerText.trim(), text, links};
}).filter(x=>/Class|OLED|QLED|Crystal|Mini LED|Micro RGB|Frame/.test(x.h)));

[38] thinking: **Parsing product cards**

I need to parse full product cards, ensuring I focus on elements like the price and rating for each. I'll spot these components using h2 tags to help me climb accurately to the necessary info on the card. It feels like a straightforward task, yet I want to make sure I don’t miss anything important! I’ll keep that in mind while I review everything carefully to avoid potential hiccups.

[39] tool_call: repl("Parsing product cards")
<request>
const cards1 = await page.locator('h2').evaluateAll(hs => hs.map((h,i)=>{
  const a = h.querySelector('a[href]');
  if (!a || !/Class/.test(h.innerText)) return null;
  let node = h.parentElement;
  let card = null;
  for (let depth=0; depth<12 && node; depth++, node=node.parentElement) {
    const t = node.innerText || '';
    if (/\$[\d,]+\.\d{2}/.test(t) && /Compare|Buy|Learn more/.test(t)) { card = node; break; }
  }
  const text = card?.innerText || '';
  const priceMatch = text.match(/\$[\d,]+\.\d{2}/);
  const ratingMatch = text.match(/\n(\d\.\d)\n\(([^)]+)\)/) || text.match(/(\d\.\d)\s*\n?\(([^)]+)\)/);
  const feature = h.parentElement?.querySelector('p')?.innerText.trim() || '';
  return {
    name: a.textContent.replace(/\s+-\s*$/,'').replace(/\s+/g,' ').trim(),
    feature,
    href: new URL(a.getAttribute('href'), location.href).href,
    price: priceMatch?.[0] || null,
    rating: ratingMatch?.[1] || null,
    reviewCount: ratingMatch?.[2] || null,
    cardText: text.slice(0,1200)
  };
}).filter(Boolean));
console.log(JSON.stringify(cards1, null, 2));
</request>

<request>
const reviewExtract1 = await page.evaluate(() => {
  const selectors = ['[class*="bv-content-review"]', '[class*="bv-content-item"]', '[data-bv-content-id]', '[class*="bv_review"]', '[class*="bv-content-core"]'];
  const out = [];
  for (const sel of selectors) {
    document.querySelectorAll(sel).forEach((el, idx) => {
      const text = (el.innerText || '').trim();
      if (text && /Helpful\?|found this review|out of 5|recommend|ago/i.test(text)) out.push({sel, idx, cls: el.className, text});
    });
  }
  // de-dupe by text
  const seen = new Set();
  return out.filter(x => { const k=x.text.slice(0,500); if(seen.has(k)) return false; seen.add(k); return true; }).slice(0,30);
});

async function getReviewsForProduct1(target) {
  const pg = await openTab(target.url);
  await snapshot(page, {interactive:true});
  let text = null;
  try {
    await page.locator('#bv-jsonld-reviews-data').waitFor({timeout: 15000});
    text = await page.locator('#bv-jsonld-reviews-data').textContent();
  } catch (e) {
    // Try clicking the reviews button if present, then read again.
    const btns = await page.locator('button').evaluateAll(btns => btns.map((b,i)=>({i, text:b.innerText||b.getAttribute('aria-label')||'', cls:b.className})).filter(x=>/review/i.test(x.text+x.cls)).slice(0,5));
    if (btns[0]) await page.locator('button').nth(btns[0].i).click().catch(()=>{});
    await page.locator('#bv-jsonld-reviews-data').waitFor({timeout: 15000});
    text = await page.locator('#bv-jsonld-reviews-data').textContent();
  }
  const data = JSON.parse(text);
  const reviews = (data.review || []).map(r => ({
    headline: r.headline || '',
    reviewBody: r.reviewBody || '',
    rating: r.reviewRating?.ratingValue ?? null,
    author: r.author?.name || '',
    datePublished: r.datePublished || r.dateCreated || '',
    images: Array.isArray(r.image) ? r.image.length : 0,
    bodyLength: (r.reviewBody || '').length
  }));
  return {...target, url: page.url(), jsonReviewCount: reviews.length, reviews};
}

  {key:'U8000F', name:'55 Inch Class Crystal UHD U8000F', url:'https://www.samsung.com/us/tvs/uhd-4k-tv/55-inch-class-crystal-uhd-u8000f-4k-smart-tv-sku-un55u8000ffxza/', listingRating:'4.5', listingReviewCount:'1,362', price:'$299.99'}
];

async function readReviewJson2(target) {
  await openTab(target.url);
  await snapshot(page, {interactive:true});
  let txt = '';
  for (let attempt = 0; attempt < 8; attempt++) {
    const count = await page.locator('#bv-jsonld-reviews-data').count();
    if (count > 0) {
      txt = await page.locator('#bv-jsonld-reviews-data').textContent();
      if (txt && txt.trim()) break;
    }
    if (attempt === 2) {
      const reviewButtonIndex = await page.locator('button').evaluateAll(btns => btns.findIndex(b => /review/i.test((b.innerText||'') + ' ' + (b.getAttribute('aria-label')||''))));
      if (reviewButtonIndex >= 0) await page.locator('button').nth(reviewButtonIndex).click().catch(()=>{});
    }
    await sleep(1500);
  }
  const parsed = txt ? JSON.parse(txt) : {review:[]};
  const reviews = (parsed.review || []).map(r => ({
    headline: r.headline || '',
    reviewBody: r.reviewBody || '',
    rating: r.reviewRating?.ratingValue ?? null,
    author: r.author?.name || '',
    datePublished: r.datePublished || r.dateCreated || '',
    images: Array.isArray(r.image) ? r.image.length : 0,
    bodyLength: (r.reviewBody || '').length
  }));
  return {...target, finalUrl: page.url(), jsonReviewCount: reviews.length, reviews};
}

const allProductReviews2 = [];
for (const target of productTargets2) {
  const res = await readReviewJson2(target);
  allProductReviews2.push(res);
}

function summarizeReviewScore2(r) {
  const body = r.reviewBody || '';
  const keywords = ['picture','sound','bright','color','contrast','setup','remote','gaming','apps','design','glare','reflection','room','value','easy'];
  const keywordHits = keywords.filter(k => body.toLowerCase().includes(k)).length;
  return (body.length || 0) + keywordHits * 50 + (r.images || 0) * 80 + (Number(r.rating) || 0) * 20;
}
const selectedReviews2 = allProductReviews2.map(p => {
  const reviews = [...p.reviews].sort((a,b)=>summarizeReviewScore2(b)-summarizeReviewScore2(a)).slice(0,3).map(r => ({...r, score:summarizeReviewScore2(r)}));
  return {key:p.key, name:p.name, price:p.price, listingRating:p.listingRating, listingReviewCount:p.listingReviewCount, url:p.finalUrl, jsonReviewCount:p.jsonReviewCount, selected:reviews};
});
console.log(JSON.stringify(selectedReviews2, null, 2));
